posted:Posted May 4, 2024
msg:I stayed in three hotels during my trip to Jiangxi, and this was the one I was most satisfied with. The hotel is on the lake, so it is quiet in the bustling city, but it takes about ten minutes to walk from the subway station. This hotel is different from the new hotel. It will not disturb you too much before the trip, but after arriving, I found that it has been arranged quite well. This time, the room type was upgraded, the floor is higher, and the scenery outside the window is beautiful. The room is full of details, and the bathtub has been prepared with disposable bath bags, so you can take a bath with peace of mind. There are 4 sets of toothbrushes and slippers. If you have a baby, you donâ€™t need to prepare them separately. Even if two people use them, sometimes the slippers are easy to get wet and can be replaced in time. After going out for a while, I came back and found that there was an extra fruit plate in the room. The swimming pool opened at 7 o'clock in the morning. It is a standard swimming pool with a suitable water temperature and a starry sky ceiling. The breakfast selection is located by the window with a good view. The standard soup noodles and clay pots for Nanchang breakfast are available, as well as special carbon water such as scallion pancakes and spring rolls. There is a coffee shop (free) on the small road along the lake outside the hotel. Friends who like to drink coffee can check in.
